People from Hunan in Beijing Discuss Methods to Relieve the Flood Disaster 131

Hunan Province has suffered from frequent disasters and is devastated. Recently, it has been hit by floods again, and telegrams of appeal have been pouring in, seeking urgent relief. Shu Chushi, the Beijing representative of the Hunan Provincial Disaster Relief Association, specially invited fellow Hunanese in Beijing yesterday to discuss relief methods and appeal to various agencies. After a unanimous decision on the spot, the following notice was issued: "Dear Sirs, unfortunately, Hunan has suffered from frequent disasters over the years. Recently, it has been plagued by major floods, and the people's livelihood is extremely destitute. Therefore, on the 5th of this month, our office invited fellow countrymen to meet and discuss relief methods. It was decided to quickly request the Ministry of Finance to allocate 100,000 yuan for urgent relief in Changsha from the previous year, and to appeal to the Central Relief Committee and the Ministry of Interior for disaster relief. Mr. He Guiyan, Lu Ju-sun, Xi Chulin, Peng Chongwei, and Shu Chushi were appointed to go to the Ministry of Finance to urge the allocation of 100,000 yuan for urgent relief. Mr. Chou Yishan, Peng Xinmin, Jiang Kecheng, Chen Mo-xi, and Shu Chushi were appointed to go to the Central Relief Committee to appeal for relief. Mr. Peng Quanfang, Zhang Muxian, Lei Shiruo, Li Zao-ying, Wang Duanmin, and Shu Chushi were appointed to go to the Ministry of Interior to plead for assistance, so as to mobilize all forces and alleviate the disaster. All the resolutions made have been specially notified by letter for your reference. Respectfully, the Beijing Office of the Hunan Provincial Disaster Relief Association."

Liu Zhenhua's Announcement to the People of Western Henan on Implementing Pacification 132

To the people of the counties of Western Henan: In recent years, affected by the current situation, the suffering of the people in Western Henan can be said to have reached its extreme. Since the end of the war last year, although order in the area has gradually recovered, incidents of bandit gangs looting villages and individual bandits robbing and seizing goods still occur everywhere. Residents are still startled several times a night, unable to live in peace at home. What a painful life this is! This Commissioner-General has moved to Luoyang this time, and is ordered to implement pacification work in Western Henan. The task undertaken is to suppress bandits and clear the countryside. Suppressing bandits is to remove the current obstacles for the people, and clearing the countryside is to seek permanent peace for the people. The phrase "cooperate with the people" is the sole purpose of this Commissioner-General. Anything that benefits the people will be done without hesitation; anyone who harms the people will be eliminated on behalf of the people. This is the first thing this Commissioner-General announces to my people. Speaking of the bandit situation in Western Henan, it is also very complex. Some are driven by hunger and cold and take risks; some are forced by circumstances and only care about the present. Still others are exploited by others, gathering vagrants, hoping to be recruited and see it as a shortcut to promotion and fortune. In summary, it can be said that only a small number of people are socially undesirable and willingly become bandits. Western Henan is this Commissioner-General's hometown, and this Commissioner-General knows the local situation and social conditions most clearly. I hope everyone will thoroughly awaken, fathers will advise and brothers will encourage, and quickly seek to extricate themselves. The ancients said, "Lay down the butcher knife and become a Buddha on the spot." If everyone knows that the path they have taken before was completely wrong, and repent wholeheartedly, this Commissioner-General will not only not pursue trivial matters or delve into the past, but will also take measures to protect them so that they can live and work in peace. This is another matter that this Commissioner-General announces to my people. Furthermore, the current social situation in Western Henan is one of poverty and exhaustion of wealth, and extreme hardship. To start construction work, we must first cultivate the vitality of the region. Eliminating violence and ensuring peace is the most important task at present. Since this Commissioner-General bears the responsibility of maintaining public order, I naturally have the determination to stabilize society. For those who have gone astray, I sincerely hope that they will reflect and ensure their safety. However, for bandits who are obsessed and harm the people, I will never dare to be lenient. I should follow the common psychological demands of the people, unite the strength of the people, and jointly defend ourselves in order to fulfill the duties that this Commissioner-General should fulfill. May my people consider this. Respectfully announced by Liu Zhenhua, Commissioner-General for Pacification of the Border Region of Henan, Shaanxi, and Shanxi.

All Sectors Organize Smoking Ban Supervision Committee 133

The Wu County Party Affairs Rectification Committee convened a joint conference of all sectors yesterday to oppose the public sale of opium. Yuan Xiaogu, Director of the Wu County Finance Bureau, requested to resign due to difficulties in handling affairs. Ten Robbers from Wujiang Apprehended 135

Xu Fengshan, a special agent of the Wujiang Water Patrol Team, in conjunction with Wuxi detectives, apprehended ten robbers, including Ji San, Chen Yushan, Ji Er, Han Jinyuan, Chen Zhengshou, Shao Siyi, Zhang Guicai, Qin Linshi, Chen Wangshi, and Chen Caishi, at Sanliqiao in Wuxi and the Qingyunge Teahouse. The Changshu County Government has received reports that there are 60 to 70 shrimp gang boats operating near Xianzi Mountain and Xiaojing, which border the county. Their movements are erratic. Ostensibly, they fish for shrimp, but in reality, they are pirate ships. Yesterday (the 7th), they specially consulted with the local county government to strictly crack down on them.

Hidden Guns Found on Straw Coffin 137

The Shanghai Zhabei Water Patrol Team previously apprehended four kidnappers, including Zhu Bolin, on a water chestnut boat in Zhenru. After interrogation, they were escorted to Qingpu. Lu of Xiezhuang Village Kidnapped 138

Lu Chunlong, a farmer in Xiezhuang Village, Fourth District, owns a small amount of land. Several bandits suddenly came to rob his house the night before last. Lu resisted and was stabbed with a bayonet, causing profuse bleeding. He fled in pain, but was captured. As a result, a man named Lu was kidnapped, and the bandits fled with shouts.

Wuxi

Killed Wife and Lied About Sudden Illness 139

Feng Dongbao, a villager in Huangjinbang near Liutanqiao, District 11 (Nanyan City), is over fifty years old and has a modest family fortune. His wife, Sima, bore him one son and three daughters. At 3:00 PM the day before yesterday, Dongbao and his wife suddenly argued over a trivial matter, which escalated into a physical fight. Dongbao, in a fit of anger, threw a clay pot from the table at his wife. It hit Sima's head, causing her to bleed profusely and faint. Shortly after, she died. The next day, Dongbao knew that he had caused a disaster and sent someone to inform the mother's family of the deceased, falsely claiming that Sima had died of a sudden illness. After receiving the news, the nephew learned that his aunt had died unnaturally, but due to poverty, he was unable to avenge his aunt and had to let her be buried hastily.

River Water Rises Sharply and Low-Lying Fields are Flooded 140

It has been raining heavily in the city for three days and nights, and the river water has risen three or four feet. The low-lying fields in the surrounding countryside have been flooded. Vegetables along the river and in low-lying areas have been submerged, causing prices to rise sharply. Watermelons in low-lying areas have also been flooded, resulting in heavy losses. Small steamships heading to Jiangyin and other places have also been suspended. Only small steamships to Nanfangquan and one or two other places are still operating normally, causing inconvenience to transportation and delays in mail. Each ship hires temporary small boats to operate, profiting from the transportation. Roads such as Youlong along the river outside the North Gate and Xiaomuqiao in the West City are all submerged in water, preventing pedestrians from passing. There are many cases of centuries-old houses collapsing due to water intrusion. The river system at Ximen Bridge is an important route to Taihu Lake.

Page 10

The river has been turbulent for days, making navigation dangerous. There have been two tragic incidents of children drowning.

Changshu Robbers Arrested in Wuxi 141

Xu Fengshan, Captain of the Detective Team of the Changshu Public Security Bureau, learned that the robbers who robbed Gu Chenbo's family in Nanchuanwei, Changshu County, were residing in this city. Yesterday, he brought a document to Wuxi and reported to the Public Security Bureau. Director Xu immediately dispatched detectives Dai Shouquan and others to cooperate with Captain Xu to make arrests. They found two awning boats under Wuqiao and apprehended the robbers Ji Zhenghua (aka Ji Er), Jiang Yunfeng (aka Ji San), Chen Wuxiao (aka Xiao Mazi), Han Jinyuan, and Chen Zhengshou. They were taken to the Public Security Bureau and temporarily detained. After the Changshu County Government's official document of detention arrives in Wuxi, they will be transferred to Changshu for investigation and prosecution.

Li Jinfang Submits Impeachment of the Finance Department to the Supervisory Yuan 143

Li Jinfang, the former Magistrate of Liyang County, reported that Pan Keping, the former Director of the County Finance Bureau, colluded with Shi Chuanji, a standing member of the Chamber of Commerce, to open a court for investigation. Pan Keping did not appear in court due to illness, and the Finance Department sent a letter to the court to prove it on his behalf. Because Pan was an employee of the Finance Department who had been suspended, the Finance Department's behavior of communicating about Pan's failure to appear in court was reported to the Supervisory Yuan, requesting impeachment. It was also stated that Pan Keping was a person selected by Jiangsu Province. According to the selection regulations, if corruption is discovered, the original recommender should be punished. The matter was referred to the National Government, instructing the original recommender and the Finance Department of Jiangsu Province to hand over Pan Keping to the case as soon as possible to avoid prolonged suspension.

Jin Haihe, a member of the Baoweituan (local defense corps) of Xincang Sanzhuhe Village in this county, colluded with Wang Sihe and his son this spring to sell five rows of bullets from the public weapons of the Baoweituan to the bandit Liu Dexing. Chen Laohu, a bandit who surrendered some time ago, reported to the Baoweituan that the Liu bandit had been killed, and the case of private sale of military weapons was also exposed. The four offenders, including Ma's son, were escorted to the county government for severe punishment in accordance with the law.

Huzhou

Cloth Industry吵盤 (chaopan- price-raising competition) Results in City-Wide Shutdown 151

There is a Dingxin Cloth Shop on Beijie (North Street) in this city. It moved from Zhicheng Road in March of this year and was scheduled to reopen on June 30. Therefore, the manager of the shop, Cheng, requested a 吵盤 for several days from the Cloth Industry Association beforehand. The industry association agreed to allow three days. Therefore, the shop hung colorful banners and put on a 吵盤 starting from the opening day. Unexpectedly, the three shops, Zenghui, Derun, and Yichengxing, also intended to sell their goods for profit and each put on their own 吵盤. As a result, the businesses that were not putting on a 吵盤 inevitably experienced sluggish business. Therefore, at around 7:00 PM yesterday the 5th, apart from the above four shops, representatives from both labor and management of the remaining shops gathered at the Cloth Industry Association for a meeting. It was resolved that, because the three-day period had expired, the 吵盤 of each shop should be stopped. Therefore, at around 7:30 AM this morning, Li, from the Tongyu Cloth Shop on Beijie (located diagonally across from Dingxin), and dozens of laborers from the industry went to the Dingxin Cloth Shop and ordered the paper banners hanging in the shop to be removed immediately. The Dingxin employees replied that they would remove them as soon as the manager arrived at the shop, etc., which led to arguments and then fights. The Public Security Bureau heard the news and immediately dispatched police officers to intervene. As a result, a man named Zhan from Tongyu Shop was injured in the face, and the counter boxes in the Dingxin Shop were overturned. All cloth shops in this city, except for the above shops putting on 吵盤, were all closed.

Hangzhou

Li Zicai's Case of Dereliction of Duty Opens for Trial 152

Li Zicai, the former Director of the Hangzhou Municipal Public Security Bureau, was found by Zhu Jiahua, Director of the Civil Affairs Department, to have violated the law and neglected his duties, embezzling nearly 20,000 yuan of public funds. Zhu arrested Li and transferred him to the court for legal punishment. After many trials, the evidence was conclusive, and he was sentenced to one year of imprisonment. Li stated that he would appeal, but because he fell ill in prison, he repeatedly requested bail. After paying a temporary bail of 17,000 yuan, Li went to Harbin to serve as secretary of the Chinese Eastern Railway Council. Therefore, the case was delayed until now, and it has been more than a year. It is now learned that the case will be heard at 10:00 AM today (the 7th) in the third criminal court of the Zhejiang High Court. The summons to Li was sent to both Li's residence in Peiping and Harbin, entrusting the courts in those locations to deliver the summons on behalf of the court. The summons to Peiping has been returned because Li was not there. There is still no news from Harbin. Therefore, Li has not appeared. The defendants in the case are Zhu Chengjie, former section chief of the Third Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and the accountant Yao Ailuo. Police were dispatched to their original residences to arrest Zhu Yao, but they were not found. Only the witness Zhu Rongtai, owner of the firewood and charcoal store Zhu Liansheng, arrived that day, and the store's books and records were retrieved for inspection by the court. Presiding Judge Wang Rulin questioned the witness, proving that the chops on the firewood and charcoal purchase invoices were indeed forged and that the amounts did not match. However, since none of the defendants were present, the court was adjourned and a new hearing date was set.

Verdict in the Longjing Kidnapping and Murder Case 153

The case of Yue merchant Li Jiyun, who was kidnapped and murdered by bandits at Longjing Temple in West Lake and whose body was dumped in the lake, has been investigated. The bandits involved in the case, Wang E, Wang Yang, Wu Jingyuan, Ying Aquan, his wife Ying Wen, Guan Zhuangren Li Wang, the fraudster Wang Fengshan, Wang Zhangshui and other nine people have been apprehended one after another. They were sent to court for punishment, and prosecuted in accordance with the Regulations for the Punishment of Kidnappers. The final hearing concluded on June 29, and the verdict was announced yesterday. Li Wang, for the crime of harboring the kidnappers, was sentenced to twelve years of imprisonment. Li Zubei, for the crime of moving the body, was sentenced to one year of imprisonment. Wang Fengshan and Wang Zhangshui, for the joint crime of fraud, were each sentenced to eight months of imprisonment. Ying Wen was found not guilty. The sentences for the four accused, Wang Yang, Wang E, Wu Jingyuan, and Ying Aquan, are temporarily suspended.

The bandit Tang Linye was sentenced to twelve years in prison by the Fenghua County Government and was serving his sentence in the Fenghua Prison. Shangyu

Banditry Rises Again at the Border of Yu and Feng 157

Pingkeng, Huixi and other villages bordering this county and Fenghua County have always been a den of bandits. Because the area is located in the mountains, connecting several counties, and both civilians and bandits live there, they carry plows and hoes during the day and go out to kidnap and loot at night. Government troops find it difficult to suppress and appease them. Although the Provincial Government dispatched security teams last winter to carry out a painful suppression for more than a month within a dozen miles around the village, the adjacent villages were able to enjoy a small degree of prosperity. However, these people are exceptionally stubborn. Banditry has been rampant again since the beginning of summer. Recently, they kidnapped a twelve-year-old "god of wealth" from a certain place in Yin County and hid him in a cave with tight security. Nearby villagers are afraid of repeating the tragedies of the past and have risen up to organize self-defense groups to guard against unexpected events.

Elementary School Teacher Registration Announced 158

The County Education Bureau held the first district registration of elementary school teachers throughout the county in May. It has now been completed. On the afternoon of the first day, a review committee was opened in the bureau to determine the validity period, which was divided into five types: two years, half a year, one year, half a year, and half a year of probation. A total of eighty-six people passed this time, including sixty-three local teachers, eight from Sheng County, four from Yuyao, four from Hang County, two from Shaoxing, two from Dongyang, one from Yongkang, one from Zhuji, and one from Yiwu. Teachers from outside the county accounted for slightly less than three-tenths. Last year, 205 people passed the registration, and teachers from outside the county accounted for more than one-third.

Xiaoshan

Sudden Major Collapse of Sand Land in Eastern Township 159

Jiangbin Dingjiang and other townships in eastern Xiaoshan, located on the Qiantang River, have experienced large tides recently, causing more than twenty miles of newly formed sand land to suddenly collapse and fall. It has now approached the old embankment, only fifty paces from the newly built embankment last year. The situation is urgent and precarious. As a result, residents along the river are in great panic and show signs of unease.

Parricide Case Occurs Outside the East Gate 160

Lou Baozhen, wife of Han Rongsheng, owner of Han Yuanchang's copper and tin shop outside the East Gate of Xiaoshan in Fan Jia Nongkou, because her husband was poor and ugly, and failed to please her, held a polyandrous point of view. On the 6th, she secretly hid saltpetre in a teapot in order to murder her husband. Fortunately, it was detected early, and no disaster occurred. The promiscuous woman has been detained for investigation.

Accusations of Extortion by Alcohol Tax Inspectors 161

Yao Jiaming, an alcohol tax inspector in Xiaoshan (erroneously reported as Yao Lie in the previous report), extorted 300 to 400 silver dollars while in the countryside. He first went to the Wendao Village Committee, and the village chief appointed Xu Songlin and others to privately extort money from door to door without issuing receipts or tickets. Then he went to Shi Yu Village and Sangjiang Village, where he also extorted hundreds of dollars. No farmer who brewed even a few dou (unit of volume) of alcohol was spared. Yesterday, the farmers of Dongcao Village also telegraphed the Provincial Bureau to request an investigation.

Order from the Jiangsu Education Department Urging the Compilation and Submission of the Education Budget Plan for the 20th Year 167

Order from the Jiangsu Education Department to the governments of Zhenjiang and 17 other counties: Regarding the education plans and budgets of the various counties for the 20th year, orders were previously issued to prepare them separately and submit them to this department for verification and instructions before March 30 of this year, and orders have been issued to urge them. Now that the 19th year has ended and the 20th year is about to begin, the education plan and budget for the 20th year in your county has not yet been submitted for verification. The progress of future undertakings and various expenditures will inevitably lack a basis. Such repeated delays are a mistake in important government affairs. Another order is hereby issued, urging the county magistrate to supervise and urge the education bureau to prepare and submit the documents to the department immediately. Before this plan and budget have been submitted and approved, the county magistrate and education bureau director shall be jointly responsible for compensating any expenditures that exceed the approved budget in the future. This order must be strictly followed.

The funding for primary schools in urban and rural areas of Wuxian County was previously only issued until the first half of May. Now, due to the end of the summer vacation and the end of the year, representatives from various schools have repeatedly urged the Education Bureau to pay. The bureau is also well aware of the difficult situation, but after exhausting all means, it managed to raise the funding for the second half of May and issued it yesterday afternoon. However, the principals of various schools believe that the teachers are poor and cannot be owed for long, so most of the funding for June has been temporarily advanced.

Local News

Regular Meeting of the Shanghai County Social Education Research Association 170

The Shanghai County Social Education Research Association held its second regular meeting yesterday at the County Education Bureau. Those present were Zhang [name missing], Jin Zuobin, Zheng Shaoyuan, Zhai Jiayou, Zhang Ji, Xu Fanliang, and Xi Langqing. Zhang Yi served as chairman, and Zhang You served as recorder. The procedures were carried out as usual. Matters reported: [omitted]. Matters discussed: (1) Regarding how to produce exhibits for the provincial social education exhibition, it was resolved that: (1) a joint request would be made to the County Education Bureau to allocate 400 yuan for exhibit materials, which would be the responsibility of the General Affairs Department of this association; (2) the County Education Bureau would be asked to select the paper for charts and graphs; (3) the County Education Bureau would be asked to select the paper for regulations and draft plans. (2) Regarding how to connect activity centers, it was resolved that after the Education Bureau drafts a plan, this association will consider the situation and hold joint events. (3) Regarding how to publicly study trial results, it was resolved that each social education organization must report the implementation situation, experiences, and difficulties of the previous month to this association during the monthly meeting for public study and discussion. (4) Regarding how to urge the payment of outstanding membership fees owed by various organizations, it was resolved that the General Affairs Department would send letters to each organization to collect the prescribed amount. (5) Regarding how to hold a summer hygiene promotion, it was resolved that: (1) the activities would include (A) exhibitions and (B) costume parades; (2) the expenses would be (A) paid from the regular expenses of this association, and if insufficient, allocated proportionally, but not exceeding 50 yuan in total; (3) the dates would be limited to one week starting from July 8; (4) the route would be Minhang, Yutang, Beiqiao, Zhuanqiao, Caohang, Tangwan, Chenhang, and Sanlin. (6) Regarding the location and date of the next meeting, it was resolved that it would be held on July 13 in the People's Education Experimental Zone. The meeting adjourned.

Jiangsu Province's Budget Proposal for Education in the 20th Year (3) By Shi Zhang 172

(3) Contents of Increased Funding for Various Educational Institutions

The general amount of the approved budget for provincial educational institutions this year and last year has been described in detail yesterday. We can understand the comparison between the two to learn that the funding for each school has almost all increased compared to last year. (The funding for Central University remains the same, with no increase or decrease. However, Central University is a national university, and it is indeed insufficient to allocate its funding from Jiangsu's education expenses. However, the Administrative Yuan's 34th meeting on August 20, the 18th year, resolved that "Central University's funding should be permanently allocated by the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office according to the fixed amount of 1,320,000 yuan in the 17th year." The provincial government has no choice but to comply with this.) As for the increased components, it is what was mentioned the day before yesterday (July 6), such as natural grade increases, etc. Now, let's briefly describe the situation.

1. In the 20th year, various primary and secondary schools need to appropriately add grades due to natural connections. It is estimated that four grades need to be added to junior high school, five grades to senior high school, six grades to rural normal school, ten grades to experimental primary school, and two grades to simple primary school, requiring a total funding of 108,000 yuan.

2. Within this year, due to curriculum modifications and increased credits in junior high schools, the original hourly fees are insufficient. Approximately 2 hours will be added to each grade in junior high schools on average, costing a total of 20,000 yuan.

3. Among provincial schools, vocational courses or vocational schools will be established appropriately in those with relatively complete facilities and special circumstances. The total equipment and start-up costs will be 30,000 yuan, of which 20,000 yuan can be transferred from the remaining funds under the special project fund for primary and secondary schools in the 19th year. The actual increase is 10,000 yuan.

4. Rural normal schools were originally a three-year system, but after being changed to a four-year system in the 17th year, grades must be added in the 20th year. The original school buildings and equipment are difficult to meet the needs and must be supplemented appropriately. An average of 5,000 yuan is estimated per school, totaling 30,000 yuan for six schools.

5. As of now, the counties north of the Yangtze River still do not have a provincial-level education center, which is a pity. In order to promote the widespread development of social education, it has been decided to add a farmer education center in Xuzhou (i.e., Tongshan County) north of the Yangtze River this year. It is heard that the regular expenses for running it will be approximately 40,000 yuan.

6. For the sake of natural connections, the College of Education needs to add four grades to each department and specialty this year, requiring at least 35,000 yuan.

7. Various social education institutions also need to increase funding due to natural development, appropriating 10,000 yuan.

8. Before the National Games in the 20th year, it is planned to hold an amateur sports meeting. The original sports meeting fee (13,000 yuan and 1,100 yuan) is insufficient, and at least 3,000 yuan needs to be added.

9. In order to step up the supervision of the education funds in various counties, the Education Fund Committee's 22nd meeting on December 9 of last year resolved to increase the number of supervisors, adding 500 yuan per month in expenses, totaling 6,000 yuan per year.

The total amount of the above nine items is 262,000 yuan. These are the largest components of increased funding for each unit. In addition, there are several small additions:

1. Increase of equipment personnel in agricultural and sericultural schools: 5,000 yuan

2. Increase of regular expenses for the National Studies Library: 3,750 yuan

3. Provincial school achievement exhibition: 3,000 yuan

4. People's schools: 3,000 yuan

5. People's education achievement exhibition: 1,500 yuan

6. Subsidy for Zhengze Middle School: 2,000 yuan

7. Subsidy for Jingzhi Girls' School: 2,000 yuan

8. Subsidy for Yutang People's Education Center: 3,000 yuan

The total of these eight items is 23,250 yuan. Combining it with the above, the total is 285,250 yuan, which is the entire component of the increase in funding. (To be continued)

Xu Kepei, Former Player of the Qingguang Basketball Team, is a Hero in France 179

Returned to China with a Master's Degree in Political Economy after Studying in France for Nearly Two Years

Experienced in More Than a Hundred Battles, He Dominated the French Basketball Scene

A Well-Rounded Player with Both Intelligence and Courage: Xu Kepei, Former Star of the Qingguang Basketball Team, Recently Returned from France. Mr. Xu Resided in France for Approximately One Year and Ten Months, Obtaining a Master's Degree in Political Economy from the University of Toulouse. When Mr. Xu First Arrived in France, He Occasionally Threw Basketballs and Was Suddenly Appreciated by the President of a Well-Known Local Sports Association, Earning a Place as One of the Official Players. Afterwards, His Fame Spread, and Everyone in the French National Basketball Community Knew of Xu Kepei, a Chinese Man Skilled in Basketball, and Adored Him. Relying on His Genuine Skills, He Represented the New Chinese Youth and Waved His Power in a Foreign Land. Xu Kepei is Truly a Good Man of the Sports World.

Obtained a Master's Degree in Political Economy in France 180

In the 18th year of the Republic of China, Mr. Xu and his classmate Wu Shengwu went to France by boat to study. Xu entered the University of Toulouse to study political economy, and Wu entered the University of Paris to study sociology. Xu continued to appear in the basketball gym in his spare time, while Wu gave up sports and focused on his textbooks. Their daily lives were different, and their personalities changed accordingly. Xu remained strong as before, while Wu became bloated like a fat man. Xu graduated on June 12 of this year with a Master's Degree in Political Economy and returned to China. Wu will return to China next spring. Wu is also a talent in the Chinese sports world, but it is a pity that he gave up halfway.

Mr. Xu Kepei

His Fame Almost Spread Throughout the National Basketball Community 181

Within three months of Mr. Xu's stay in France, he was invited by the famous Toulouse CA Colonne to sign up and join the basketball team, earning a place as one of the official players. The school basketball team lost a strong player, which was regrettable at the time. Mr. Xu has experienced more than a hundred battles, and the most memorable ones were the Southwest Provinces Open League, the Big City League, and the French National Championship. The Toulouse team won the championship in the first two competitions, and Xu, as the captain of the team, made great contributions. In the last competition, they were defeated by the Paris team in the semi-finals. Xu's great talent and fame were spread through these three major competitions. Afterwards, many basketball teams invited him to serve as an honorary coach. Xu was unable to refuse and accepted the position in his spare time, also serving as a coach for a women's team in Bordeaux. The women in that area used the same rules as men, were lively and brave, and sometimes even surpassed men. As for the sports situation in France, tennis and American football are very popular. After the Four Musketeers kept the World Davis Cup Tennis Championship for several times, the national atmosphere became more intense. The level of basketball is also very average. If an excellent Chinese team can be organized, it will not be difficult to sweep across European countries. There is a lack of sports organizations among students studying in France, so this can also be reported.

In the future, in addition to serving as a teacher at a certain university, Mr. Xu will still be active in the basketball world when he has time. Mr. Xu has not yet formally indicated whether he will serve the Qingguang team again.

New York, 5th—Official Molton, the secretary of the New York Athletic Association, formally announced today that the World Heavyweight Boxing Championship has not yet been decided in New York. Free Talk

World Anecdotes 186

— Hai Ke

The Lorgnette of Fashionable Women

Modern fashionable women do not like to wear glasses, thinking that wearing glasses is a sign of being unfashionable. Therefore, many fashionable women, even if their eyesight is poor, reluctantly socialize and never resort to glasses. However, in the social circles of England in 1929, a type of lorgnette became popular. Generally, fashionable women all have a lorgnette propped on their eyes. They are all made of clear glass, said to enhance beauty. But it is not easy to prop a lorgnette on the eyes. Inadvertently, it often falls off. So they have to be careful and vigilant, as if they have one more thing to worry about. Examining the history of the lorgnette, it was first discovered in 1815. At the congress in Vienna, Austria, there was a diplomat who was the first to wear the lorgnette. After that, gentlemen and beautiful young men from various European countries followed suit. Unexpectedly, more than a hundred years later, it has become an ornament for fashionable women in England again.

The Language of Thieves

In the world, no matter which country they are from, all good looters and petty people have their own unique language. Outsiders do not know it. The lower classes of Chinese society are the same, and it is called “Qie Kou” (slang). Now, there are a group of clever thieves in Europe who have newly invented an internationally used language, specifically for their use. Because their party includes people from England, France, America, Germany, Italy, Spain, Portugal, and Greece, they cannot understand each other, which is extremely inconvenient. Therefore, there must be a commonly used world language. Recently, due to the cracking of a major case, a notebook was found, and it was then discovered that there was this newly invented world language of thieves. It is said that in recent years, there have been many unsolved mystery cases that are the masterpiece of this criminal gang.

A Sketch of the Gansu Disaster 187

— Sun Choucheng

The situation in Gansu is extremely dire, and the people are struggling to survive, even eating elm bark and alfalfa to fill their stomachs. For the past five years, natural and man-made disasters have been pressing down on them. Because it is located in a remote border area with dangerous roads, relief workers are hesitant to move forward. In addition, they have long been under the oppressive power of warlords, and the situation is constrained, making it impossible to appeal for help. The true picture of the disaster has not been fully disclosed and made known to the people of the country, which is extremely heartbreaking. Recently, an old friend, Mr. Mou, came to Shanghai from Gansu and showed me his recent works on eating elm bark and alfalfa, etc. Each word is filled with tears, making it unbearable to read. I am transcribing it for this column and publicizing it on his behalf. I believe that benevolent gentlemen will also approve.

(Eating Elm Bark) Eating elm bark alleviates poverty and hunger, sometimes like roasting fragrant tea, splitting it into pieces like purple Ganoderma, or like grinding and stir-frying flour, making cakes better than minced meat. Scrape the frost off the elm tree with a sharp blade. Plants seem to know, enduring the pain of having their skin peeled and flesh cut away, just to feed the people and enrich their fat. The hungry stomach rumbles like a turning pulley, leaning against the tree twelve hours a day. The old elm tree stands tall, sacrificing itself to help people without complaint. The craftsman turns away, laughing at the elm tree covered in sores. The elm tree cannot speak, but it is cut down. The tree sways in the wind, whimpering. The craftsman laughs at my foolishness; I laugh at the craftsman's ignorance. I not only willingly shed my skin and flesh for people to chew, but also scatter copper coins to help people in times of crisis. The tree is like this; what about people? They retaliate with mockery and criticism, refusing to cure chronic illnesses with arrogance and stinginess. Hoarding wealth leads to destruction; heaven is not deceived. It is cruel not to be a benevolent teacher. Is it right for the many to be poor while the few are rich? Eating peach pits, indulging in jest, let us forget about it. When the elm tree cries out triumphantly, I hear tears like silk. Must one have wealth to help the world? When will a thousand granaries and ten thousand storehouses fill the void? Must one have position to save the country? Who can rely on scholars to assist the world and govern the people? It is better to follow and relieve the urgent needs, offering food and clothing to the weak and weary. Every bit of thread, every inch of cloth, every handful of rice, accumulating good deeds brings blessings; what is there to doubt? Do you not see ants carrying a thousand catties, each doing their best without fault? Do not laugh at the old elm tree as a money tree; the old elm tree scorns the obsession with money. Heavenly winds scatter elm coins, nourishing the poor children morning and evening. Poor children play, breaking branches. When the branches are broken, blood drips. Sharpening knives, they head towards the tree, diminishing it day by day, making it weak. Weak, alleviating poverty and hunger. Alleviating poverty and hunger, eating elm bark. (Alfalfa) Poor women in Tao River area gather alfalfa. Three or five female companions plan to fill their stomachs. Han fields are desolate, Hui fields are lush. Hunger drives us to compete. One catty of alfalfa costs one hundred and six coins. Hui people cherish it like wheat and beans. They cannot be stopped, they whip and beat each other. They snatch shovels and trample on baskets, retaliating quickly. Poor women flee, crying. One middle-aged wife lies stiff and prostrate. (Niansheng Gui's wife is seriously injured and unable to get up.) They kick her with old fists. Blood and bruises spread across her flesh. The injury is so severe that it is difficult to recover her vitality. Her life or death is unknown in the ditch. Poor people protect their food; who can blame them? They hate the landlords with houses full of grain. In ancient times, benevolence extended to plants and trees. Today, people are stingy and unwilling to share even thin gruel. The many are poor while the few are rich, hoarding for nine years. Being rich without benevolence does not accumulate blessings. I hear the hair standing on end, and I cut paper into strips. I urge the county magistrate to punish the wealthy families, so that the hungry people can be nourished and the greedy people will not hoard in the valleys. Hunger and drowning weigh on my mind, reading letters and lodging. Before half of the poem is written, tears fill my eyes. I will take it back to tell the pastor. I expect him to be heartbroken and unable to read it.

What is the Pleasure of Dancing? 188

— Le

In recent years, the dance craze has flourished in Shanghai. Every time the lights come on, handsome men and beautiful women gather, dancing gracefully to the music, embracing each other tightly. This joy is something outsiders cannot understand. However, since this trend has become popular, many young people have become addicted to it. A group of glamorous women haunt these places, using their seductive skills to captivate the masses and draw them into their trap. From then on, the entertainment venues have transformed into money-devouring dens, where people are known to lose their fortunes and their jobs. The wings of love are broken, and danger lurks everywhere. The authorities are indulging in pleasure and luxury, unaware that in a blink of an eye, they have fallen to an irredeemable state. Concerned individuals worry about it. Recently, it has been heard that the Star Motion Picture Company's sound film "Such is Paradise" uses the dance floor as a background and deeply depicts it, which is thought-provoking and awakens people from their dreams. It is truly a work that benefits the world and people's hearts, and it can be a warning to those who are obsessed with the dance floor.

The Problem of Diet in Hot Weather 189

— Zui Chi Sheng

Since ancient times, our country has paid the most attention to "hygiene." The one who emphasizes this the most should be Confucius. Think about how he “would not eat wine and dried meat bought from the market.” How careful he was about diet. Because the food bought is often poorly prepared and infested with mosquitoes and flies, it is inevitably unclean. It is best not to eat it. Therefore, there is a saying, “What the eye does not see is clean.” If you were to see it with your own eyes, I guarantee you would shake your head and frown, and it would be difficult to swallow. It would indeed be a little scary. Now, I will write down a few of the "scary" situations so that people must pay extra attention to what they eat in the hot weather. The owners of the restaurants must strive to improve their hygiene facilities and must not be stubborn and muddle through, doing that "indirect murder."

Living Things in Roast Duck The day before yesterday, during lunch, I added a roast duck dish at a Muslim restaurant. Although it was an overly sensual duck, it was quite tasty to chew on carefully. Unexpectedly, after eating more than half of it, I suddenly saw something wriggling in the gravy. Upon closer inspection, it turned out to be maggots. This was a major setback. I quickly put down my chopsticks and stopped eating, and my stomach was still uneasy. As for where these maggots came from, of course, the duck had a love affair with the red-shifted flies. In addition to transmitting germs, the flies also produce white eggs. These eggs, after a few hours or exposure to sunlight, will turn into maggots. The store did not take precautions beforehand and turned a blind eye afterward, continuing to sell it to people. Imagine how hateful that is.

Special Dragon and Tiger Dish I remember last summer, one night, a few friends and I went to a famous restaurant for dinner. Everyone gorged themselves and had a great time. Later, after the soup was finished, a clear stewed whole duck was served. Everyone ate with relish. Unexpectedly, a gecko was suddenly found in the soup. Everyone was shocked. They called the manager to question him, saying that they had never tasted gecko stewed duck. The man apologized repeatedly and even deducted the price of the duck to settle the matter. I also interjected jokingly, saying that Guangzhou food includes dragon and phoenix gatherings and dragon and tiger dishes. This gecko has the shape of a dragon and the name of a tiger. It can be called a special dragon and tiger dish.

Dried Mushrooms Started Growing Legs One day, a friend and I went to a vegetarian restaurant to eat. We ordered dried mushroom noodles. My friend put on his old glasses and ate with relish. Finally, he clamped a dried mushroom and was about to put it in his mouth when he suddenly froze. He shouted, "Dried mushrooms have started growing legs!" I looked at it. It turned out to be a very large cockroach. The friend then asked the waiter, "Is this noodle vegetarian or non-vegetarian?" The waiter answered very sincerely, "No meat is allowed inside here. Of course, it is vegetarian." The friend said, "Since it is vegetarian, why add this thing inside? My vision has always been halved, and I thought it was a dried mushroom. Are your chefs the same as me?" The waiter had nothing to say and repeatedly apologized. I laughed, saying, "Dried mushrooms growing legs is a joke in a vegetarian restaurant."

A Record of the Shanghai Municipal Government's New Building Laying Ceremony 190

— Ji Ping

Yesterday, the Shanghai Municipal Government held the laying ceremony for its new building in the downtown area. This marks the beginning of the Great Shanghai Plan, and its commemoration has profound significance. I also went to watch it and see the situation. We traveled from the Park Shooting Range via the West Sports Association Road, Xiangyin Road, Songhu Road, and Sanmin Road to reach the venue. It was more than ten miles from Shanghai City, and the drive took forty minutes. The trees planted along the road were lush and green, and the road surface was paved with coal ash, which was still relatively smooth. The width was comparable to Nanjing Road. Upon reaching the venue, we saw castle-like archways facing each other to the east and west, which were quite spectacular. To the right of the entrance was the registration area for guests. The receptionist gave us a copy of this issue of the newspaper’s pictorial (because it contained the Great Shanghai film) and an overview of the Shanghai Municipal Central Area Plan. Continuing forward was the venue, a large mat shed that could accommodate 3,000 people. There were two reception rooms, one Western and one Chinese, on the left and right. To the east of the venue were the Health Bureau and staff rest rooms. To the west were two rooms displaying various drawings and models of the Great Shanghai Plan. The production was exquisite, and the planning was detailed. It was not easy to gather artists and engineers to devote their efforts and spend so much effort to create these crystallizations. However, the spiritual and material resources required to realize these various plans will be ten or a hundred times greater.

At ten o'clock, the meeting began with music. Chinese and foreign guests, men and women, were like clouds, no less than two thousand people. The distinguished guests gathered on the stage, and ordinary guests and municipal government officials stood in front of the stage, listening quietly to the great theories. However, due to the light rain, the accumulated water was an inch deep, and almost all the reeds in the field were stained by the dirty water. In several places on the west side, the water was ankle-deep. Someone called it West Lake, which shows how difficult it was to stand. After the ceremony, Mayor Zhang delivered a sincere opening speech, hoping that the central area could be transformed from a desolate land into a prosperous market. Therefore, all administrative, industrial, commercial, and transportation terminals and stations in the Great Shanghai Plan refer to the facilities of various capital cities in order to adapt to modern trends and the needs of citizens. He also said that the central area is the center of the entire Shanghai and should be supported by the efforts of all Shanghai citizens in order to succeed. In his speech, he praised former Mayor Huang Yingbai's enthusiasm for this plan and hoped to hear a word from him. Huang then took the stage to speak after the Director of Public Works, Shen Yi, reported on the preparations. The entire speech was both serious and humorous, arousing the sympathy of the entire audience. He said that Shanghai has a population of three million, which is equal to that of Xinjiang Province. He said that Shanghai's position is important because it is the gateway to the Yangtze River and the barrier to the southeast. It is both a commercial port and a military port. He said that the prosperity of the concession is praised as a medium for Western civilization, and it is destroyed as a tubercle bacillus of China's lung disease. He has a clear understanding of the corrupt phenomenon of the concession in the past eighty years. He hopes that the Great Shanghai will succeed not only in material facilities but also in the spiritual aspects of culture, morality, discipline, and order. Finally, he said that his term as mayor was very short, and all the plans he proposed were just bubbles, empty talk, equivalent to blank checks issued by the bank. Fortunately, Mayor Zhang was able to maintain his credit and cash them, which made the entire audience laugh. Then, Yu Qiaqing, Ye Gongchuo, Wang Xiaolai, and others gave speeches. Wang said that the Shanghai Concession has a history of more than eighty years, like an old and useless person. The Municipal Government is only four years old and will be a promising young man in the future. He hopes that the mayor will complete the Great Shanghai Plan, that the directors of various bureaus and the business and financial sectors will help him complete it, and that the people will urge him to complete it. His words were also very pleasant to hear. At this point, the laying ceremony was held. The mayor held the central area map, plan overview, and business report of the district construction committee, and seven or eight other books were sealed in a purple copper box and embedded in the cornerstone. The cornerstone was slowly placed, and the grand ceremony was completed.

Rotary Club Fiction

??? (15) 191

— Xu Zhuodai

Zi Liang couldn't help but be surprised when he saw it. Sure enough, under the heading of "Stir-fried Shredded Tofu with Pork," there was an item for vinegar in the ingredients list, and it was indeed written as "one tael." The usage of vinegar was also very detailed. Zi Liang was naturally puzzled. He looked at it for a long time before finally discovering a mystery.

"How come your lecture notes skip from page 45 to page 47?"

Hearing this, the lady's eyes flashed, and she also seemed very surprised. She came over to take a closer look herself and confirmed that page 46 was indeed missing.

"Blind faith in books is worse than having no books at all! You really know how to use lecture notes blindly! It's missing a page, and you still treat it like a treasure. Page 45 only has three lines about stir-fried shredded tofu with pork, and then it jumps to page 47. Who knows what it's talking about? You just randomly attach it to the stir-fried shredded tofu with pork. Adding vinegar will naturally make it inedible."

"Who would have thought it would be missing a page?"

The two finished their meal reluctantly. Zi Liang didn't dare to delay. He washed his face, grabbed a few toothpicks, and went back upstairs. After all, it wasn't convenient to immediately sit down at the table and work after eating. He needed to rest and recharge. If he stayed downstairs, he would only be bothered by her, so he temporarily escaped to his own territory.

After he went upstairs, he wanted to drink a cup of tea, but he didn't want to go back downstairs, and he was worried that the lady would insist on bringing it up herself, so he decided not to drink it after all.

He paced around in the small space of his attic, sometimes sitting down to read a book on the table. He suddenly remembered: Where's today's newspaper? Why hasn't it been brought up? He didn't want to ask, as it was better to have one less thing to worry about, so he just wouldn't read it.

After resting for a while, he was about to start working, grinding the ink and preparing to write. He'd been constantly disturbed by her in the morning, only managing to correct three books. There were still about 160 books left. How could he possibly finish them today? Just then, there were footsteps on the stairs. The lady was coming again, holding a new notebook in her hand.

Dealers from thin indica rice villages sold several hundred dan, with prices similar to the previous day. The Du Bu sharp rice also weakened today, with a sudden decline in sales and a decrease of 1.5 chi. The sales of imported sharp rice were two-fold, with prices unchanged. There was still a large supply of glutinous rice, with no transactions and a soft price trend. River factories offered about 2,600 to 2,700 dan of various goods.

Hu Nan 218

Yesterday, 21-22 ships arrived from the Pu River. The most transactions were for thin indica rice in urban and rural areas, with stable prices. There was little interest in Changzhou-Wuxi thick japonica rice and Suzhou-Tongzhou white japonica rice. It was impossible to sell Pingwang and Li Li rice without lowering the price. The sales of early rice from Tinglin and Ye Xie were especially sluggish, with prices discounted by about 1 chi. There was still a small number of customers interested in imported Du sharp rice, and the market had stabilized. Passenger sharp rice was affected by imported rice, with prices discounted by about 1 chi. Yin Yuan arrived in large quantities, and sales continued actively, with prices holding steady. There was a lack of incoming Saigon rice, with some inventory remaining. The weather turned sunny, and local sales were poor, resulting in a lower outlook.

Flour and Wheat Both Trend Weak 219

Flour 220

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the prices for various months were generally stable. Although foreign wheat continued to decrease slightly by 0.3 qian, the gold price rebounded. Although the weather was sunny, it was unusually hot and humid, and there was concern that it would rain, so the market remained stable with little fluctuation. After the opening in the afternoon, due to the still good weather, the sentiment of the domestic groups softened. Moreover, a certain factory slightly reduced its holdings recently, and the market became even quieter. The actual sales at present feel particularly quiet, and even the spot sales in Tianjin are inferior to those of previous years. The future changes should not deviate from this. As a result, the current month was down 5 li from the previous day, August, September, and October were down 1 fen, November and December were down 1 fen and 2.5 li, and December was down 1 fen, it was said.

Wheat 221

Yesterday, the futures wheat market showed a weakening trend for each month in the morning and afternoon openings. The weather had cleared, and the quoted price of foreign wheat continued to decrease by about 0.3 qian. The oversupply of foreign wheat production still did not improve due to the exchange rate. The market sentiment naturally changed again. Moreover, since the harvest of new wheat, the Shanghai factory has always been watching and has not made large-scale purchases. This situation has never happened in previous years, and the nervous sentiment had to soften. As a result, the current month was down 4 fen from the previous day, August was down 2 fen, and other months were each down 1 fen. The spot wheat market remained quiet, and major factories did not pay attention. Yesterday, more than 1,200 bags of Liuhe, Chuzhou, and Nanjing wheat were opened, and Xin Da handled it, it was said.

Silk and Tea: Summer Silkworm Arrivals in Yu Hang Become Increasingly Scarce 222

Continuous Heavy Rain...Almost to the Point of Having Sales but No Market

The early batches of summer silkworms in the four towns of Yu Hang this year were mostly abandoned, so they supplemented with late silkworms. The harvest was still poor, with an overall yield of no more than 40%. New cocoons went on the market at 56 yuan, and arrivals were not strong. Various firms competed to collect high-quality cocoons, and the price of improved silkworm eggs had already opened at 52 yuan. Continuous heavy rain prevented villagers from bringing cocoons to the market to sell, and arrivals in the market became increasingly scarce, almost to the point of having sales but no market. Cocoon prices are expected to rise by 23 yuan, it was said.

Ping Shui Green Tea Sales to Europe Turn Brisk 223

Yesterday, the Lake Chou and Ping Shui Green tea market at the local foreign firms' tea market saw sales to Europe become brisk. The total sales for the entire market, including shrimp eyes, sesame pearls, needle eyebrows, and show eyebrows, were over 4,700 boxes. The selling price was unchanged from before. Lu Zhuang's precious eyebrows, needle eyebrows, and other green teas were also purchased by Xie He, Bao Chang, and other firms. The market was slightly active. Only the China Tea Company exclusively purchased Keemun black tea, and foreign firms were still watching. The market situation was quite quiet, it was said.

Hardware: 70-80 Barrels of New Iron Wire Delivered Yesterday 224

The transaction of new iron wire suddenly had a vigorous trend yesterday. A total of 70-80 barrels were transacted, and the market price was 14 taels and 2.5 qian per box. Although there was no increase or decrease from the previous price, the internal situation was more robust than before. It was heard that the buyers were all customers from the Yangtze River area, and various groups in Tianjin and Yantai have also been inquiring recently. According to industry insiders, the current inventory is not large, and the market may have hopes of rising in the future, it was said.

Miscellaneous News: More Than 900 Pieces of Pigments Shipped from America 225

300,000 yuan in spot foreign currency was shipped to Hankou.

4,270 boxes of tea leaves were shipped to Russia.

4,000 bags of Japanese sugar were imported yesterday.

2,000 bags of sesame seeds were shipped to Italy.
